# <a name="obsolete-members-in-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="b02a1-102">Zastaralé členy v rozhraní .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b02a1-102">Obsolete members in .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b02a1-103">Tento článek uvádí členy typu, které jsou zastaralé v rozhraní .NET Framework 4.5 a novějších verzích.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b02a1-103">This article list the type members that are obsolete in .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b02a1-104">Členové typu jsou seskupeni podle sestavení.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b02a1-104">Type members are grouped by assembly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="b02a1-105">Tento článek neuvádí členy zastaralých typů.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b02a1-105">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="b02a1-106">Seznam zastaralých typů naleznete v tématu [Zastaralé typy](obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="b02a1-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>
